Pierce County, WA
Contact: Eric Lynn <kenshi634@gmail.com>
System: Firecom
These text messages are generated by a Gig Harbor firefighter who takes the dispatch messages from FireCom and send them out as text messages to subscribers. That's why there's advertisements at the bottom of each dispatch message. The general location filter in your app generally works okay on these addresses except for the intersections and the street courts or avenue courts (ex. 15821 54th st ct e). The "ct" gets cut off and google maps pulls up 54th st instead. The ",22" at the end of the address just shows the fire district and is not actually part of the address. These are all dispatches for East Pierce Fire & Rescue (district #22). 

I've found CadPage to be potentially really useful. Right now I'm still copying the address from the text message and then opening google maps and pasting the address as another way to confirm where I'm going. Using the Map feature from CadPage right now can potentially send me to the wrong place if I'm not paying attention. But if you can filter it correctly, that would be a great help to those of us who would like to use CadPage. Of course, I would gladly make a donation. Thank you.

Sample dispatches:

FIRE911

29B4 @ 16:07:45
MVA
112TH ST E / SOUTH PRAIRIE RD E,22
Map=449,RD=22- 121
to: F22

m.textmarks.com

*R u a patient? Get help ht

FIRE911

26A8 @ 08:35:14
